	color={ 160 40 40 }

	}

		if = {

		}
	}

e_roman_britannia = {
	color={ 210 90 45 }
	
	capital = c_londinium
	definite_form = yes
	
	de_jure_drift_disabled = yes
	can_be_named_after_dynasty = no

	can_create = {
		always = no			# TODO
	}
	
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_cultural_pillar = heritage_latin
			}
			add = @always_primary_score
		}
	}
			
	cultural_names = {
		name_list_french = cn_britannia_french
		name_list_norman = cn_britannia_norman
		name_list_occitan = cn_britannia_occitan
